　　论曰：阳明病下血讝语者，此为热入血室，是兼男女而言也。曰妇人中风七八日，续得寒热，发作有时，经水适断者，此为热入血室，其血必结，故使如疟状，发作有时，小柴胡汤主之。曰妇人中风，脉迟身凉，而证如结胸者，当刺期门。曰妇人伤寒经水适来，昼日明了，暮则讝语者，无犯胃气及上二焦，必自愈。按血室者，即冲任血海也，亦血分也。凡血分之病，有畜血者，以血因热结而留畜不行也。有热入血室者，以邪入血分而血乱不调也。故血畜者去之则愈，血乱者调之则安。调之之法，热者宜凉，陷者宜举，虚者宜滋，瘀者宜行，邪未散者宜解。然此皆病在下焦，故曰无犯胃气及上二焦，必自愈，是又不可不察。[101p]

The discussion states: When Yangming syndrome presents with bloody stools and aberrant speech, this is due to heat entering the blood chamber, applicable to both men and women. It mentions that if a woman experiences a stroke and then, after seven or eight days, has a recurrence of cold and heat with intermittent symptoms, accompanied by a disruption in menstrual flow, this is heat entering the blood chamber, leading to blood stagnation, which can present like a febrile disease with recurrent symptoms. Minor Chaihu Decoction is indicated for this condition.

If a woman suffers from a stroke, with a slow pulse and cool body, showing symptoms of chest blockage, she should undergo puncturing at the Qimen point. If a woman with cold-induced illness has her menstrual flow arrive at the right time, feels clear during the day but exhibits aberrant speech in the evening, she must not disturb the stomach qi or the upper two jiaos, and she will surely recover on her own.

The blood chamber refers to the Chong and Ren vessels, and also pertains to the blood division. In general, ailments of the blood division involve blood stagnation resulting from heat causing retention, or heat entering the blood chamber leading to chaotic blood flow. Thus, if the blood is stagnant, its removal will lead to recovery; if the blood is chaotic, its regulation will provide peace.

The methods for regulation are such that overheating conditions should receive cooling treatment, sinking conditions should be raised, deficient conditions should be nourished, and stagnant conditions should be moved. If the pathogenic factor has not dispersed, it should be resolved. However, all these ailments reside in the lower jiao, hence it is said not to disturb the stomach qi or the upper two jiaos; only then will recovery be assured. This must not be overlooked.[101p]

　　抵当汤 【《金匮》，下同】　治妇人经水不利。　　水蛭熬　蝱虫各三十枚，熬，去翅足　桃仁二十个，去皮尖　大黄三两，酒浸　　右四味为未，以水五升，煮取三升，去滓，温服一升。

Prescription

For treating women with difficulties in menstruation:

  1. Leech Decoction: Take 30 leeches and 30 hibiscus insects, boil them and remove wings and legs. Add 20 peach kernels (peeled and demarcated) and 3 taels of rhubarb soaked in wine. Mix these four ingredients and use five liters of water to boil until you obtain three liters, then strain. Warm and serve one liter.

  2. Alum Pill: For treating difficulties in menstruation, persistent hardened conditions, and clotted blood with white discharge. Take 5/3 taels of alum, burn it, and add 1 tael of apricot kernels. Grind these two ingredients into a powder, mix with honey, and form into pills the size of jujube pits. For severe cases, take an additional dose.[102p]

　　小柴胡汤　治妇人经病问，用此加减。　　柴胡半斤　人参去芦　甘草　生姜各三两　半夏半升　黄芩三两　大枣十二枚　　右以水一斗二升，煮取六升，去滓，再煮取三升，温服一升，日三服。
　　杏仁汤 【《千金方》，下同】　治月经不调，或一月再来，或两月三月一来，或月前或月后闭塞不通。　　杏仁二两　桃仁一两　大黄三两　水蛭　蝱虫各三十个　　右五味(口父)咀，以水六升，煮取二升，分三服。一服当有物随大小便有所下，下多者止之，少者尽三服方止。
　　大黄石卜)硝汤　治经年月水不利，胞中有风冷所致，宜下之。　　大黄　牛膝各五两　代赭一两　(石卜)硝　牡丹皮　甘草　紫菀各三两　桃仁　蝱虫　水蛭　干姜　细辛　芒硝各二两　麻仁五合　　右十四味(口父)咀，以水一斗五升，煮取五升，去滓，内硝令烊，分五服，五更为首，相去一炊顷自下，后将息。忌见风。[103p]

Xiao Chai Hu Decoction
For treating women's menstrual disorders, adjustments can be made to this recipe.

  • Chai Hu: 250 grams
  • Ren Shen (ginseng) (peel removed): 150 grams
  • Gan Cao (licorice): 150 grams
  • Sheng Jiang (fresh ginger): 150 grams
  • Ban Xia (pinellia): 250 milliliters
  • Huang Qin (scutellaria): 150 grams
  • Da Zao (jujube): 12 pieces
    Combine with 12 liters of water, boil to obtain 6 liters, strain, and boil again to get 3 liters. Warmly take 1 liter, three times a day.

Apricot Kernel Decoction
For irregular menstruation, whether it comes again in a month, or every two to three months, or be delayed before or after the expected date.

  • Xing Ren (apricot kernel): 100 grams
  • Tao Ren (peach kernel): 50 grams
  • Da Huang (rhubarb): 150 grams
  • Water leeches: 30 pieces
  • Chuan Wu (prepared earthworm): 30 pieces
    Crush the above five ingredients, use 6 liters of water to boil down to 2 liters, and divide into three doses. One dose should cause a bowel movement. If the output is excessive, stop using; if insufficient, finish three doses before stopping.

Da Huang Shi Wei Xie Decoction
For treating menstrual problems and obstruction due to cold wind in the uterus.

  • Da Huang (rhubarb): 250 grams
  • Niu Xi (achyranthes): 250 grams
  • Dai Zhe Shi (dragons blood stone): 50 grams
  • Shi Wei xiao (natural mineral salt): 150 grams
  • Mu Dan Pi (peony bark): 150 grams
  • Gan Cao (licorice): 150 grams
  • Zi Wan (aster): 150 grams
  • Tao Ren (peach kernel): 100 grams
  • Chuan Wu (prepared earthworm): 30 pieces
  • Shui Li (water leeches): 30 pieces
  • Gan Jiang (dried ginger): 100 grams
  • Xi Xin (asarum): 100 grams
  • Mang Xiao (natural saline): 100 grams
  • Ma Ren (flaxseed): 250 grams
    Crush all fourteen ingredients, boil with 15 liters of water to obtain 5 liters. Strain, then add the salines to dissolve. Divide into five doses, take the first dose at the fifth watch of the night, allowing the rest to take effect after a short while. Avoid exposure to wind.[103p]

　　茱萸蝱虫汤　治久寒月经不利，或多或少。　　吴萸三升　蝱虫　水蛭　(上庶下虫)虫　牡丹皮各一两　生姜一片　小麦　半夏各一升　桃仁五十枚　人参　牛膝各三两　桂心六两　甘草一两半　芍药二两　大枣二十枚　　右(口父)咀，以酒一斗，水二斗，煮取一斗，去滓，适寒温，一服一升，日三。不能饮酒人，以水代之。汤欲成，乃内诸虫。不耐药者，饮七合。

Zhuyukou Insect Decoction: Treats prolonged cold affecting menstrual flow, whether excessive or insufficient.

Ingredients:

  • 3 sheng of Wu Yu
  • Insect (Huang Chong)
  • Hirudo (water-leech)
  • Insects (quantity not specified)
  • 1 liang of peony root
  • 1 slice of fresh ginger
  • 1 sheng each of wheat and pinellia
  • 50 pieces of peach kernels
  • 3 liang each of ginseng and ox knee
  • 6 liang of cinnamon heart
  • 1.5 liang of licorice
  • 2 liang of peony root
  • 20 red dates

Preparation: Grind the ingredients together and mix with 1 dou of wine and 2 dou of water. Boil to extract 1 dou, remove the residue, adjust to warm temperature, and take 1 sheng as a dose, three times a day. For those who cannot drink wine, substitute with water. Add the insects just before the decoction is complete. If the patient cannot tolerate the medicine, drink 1.5 cups.

Didao Decoction: Treats menstrual flow issues, abdominal fullness, and intermittent reduction.

Ingredients:

  • 2 liang of tiger palm
  • 2 liang of dahuang (rhubarb)
  • 30 peach kernels
  • 20 leeches

Preparation: Combine these four ingredients with 3 sheng of water, boil to extract 1 sheng, and take the entire amount at once to eliminate stagnant blood.

Qiao'ao Pills: Treats menstrual issues, heat in hands and feet, abdominal fullness, lethargy, and irritability.

Ingredients:

  • 5 liang each of Qianhu and mangxiao (glauber's salt)
  • 6 zhu each of tinglei and shupepper
  • 15 zhu of fresh ginger
  • 15 zhu of feiqing (a type of fragrant herb)
  • 9 zhu of apricot kernels, processed
  • 20 peach kernels, processed
  • 1/2 he of leeches, processed
  • 1.5 liang of dahuang

Preparation: Grind the eleven ingredients into a fine powder, form into pills the size of walnuts, and take 7 pills on an empty stomach, three times a day. If uncertain, increase the amount to double. A variation of the formula omits feiqing and qianhu, substituting with ch bitrate. Another variation includes 2 liang each of hou chong and dan pi (moutan root).[104p]

The above ten ingredients, distilled with 1 dou of water, boil down to 3 sheng and 2 ge, divide into four doses, three by day and one by night.[106p]

　　黄苓牡丹汤　治女人从小至大，月经未尝来，颜色痿黄，气力衰少，饮食无味。　　黄芩　丹皮　桃仁　瞿麦　芎藭各二两　芍药　枳实　射干　海藻　大黄各一两　蝱虫七十枚　水蛭五十枚　蛴螬十枚　　右(口父)咀，以水一斗，煮取三升，分三服。服两剂后，灸乳下一寸黑员际各五十壮。
　　牡丹圆　治妇人女子，病后月经闭绝不通，及从来不通。　　瞿麦　芎藭　海藻各一两　丹皮三两　芍药　元参　桃仁　当归　桂心各二两　蝱虫　水蛭各三十枚　蛴螬二十枚　　右为末，蜜和丸梧子大，酒下十五丸，加至二十丸。如血盛者，作散服方寸匕。腹中当转如沸，血自化成水去。如小便赤少，除桂心，用地肤子一两。

Huangling Peony Decoction: This treats women who have never experienced menstruation from childhood to adulthood. They have a sallow complexion, little energy, and tastelessness in food. The ingredients include 2 liang each of Huangqin, Danpi, Taoren, Qumai, and Chuangxiong; 1 liang each of Shaoyao, Zhishi, Shegan, Haizao, and Dahuang; 70 pieces of Wucong and 50 pieces of Shuiti; and 10 pieces of Qichong. Grind the ingredients, boil them in 10 dou of water to obtain 3 sheng, and divide into three doses. After taking two doses, perform moxibustion on the area one inch below the nipple with 50 moxa sticks each.

Peony Pill: This treats women whose menstruation has ceased after illness or has never been regular. The ingredients include 1 liang each of Qumai, Chuangxiong, and Haizao; 3 liang of Danpi; 2 liang each of Shaoyao, Yuanshen, Taoren, Danggui, and Guixin; 30 pieces of Wucong and Shuiti; and 20 pieces of Qichong. Grind these into powder, mix with honey to form pills the size of a walnut, and take 15 pills with wine, up to 20 pills. If there is excessive blood, create a powder and take a spoonful. The abdomen should feel like it’s boiling, and blood should transform and flow away. If urination is scant and red, replace Guixin with 1 liang of Difuzi.

Dried Lacquer Pill: This treats menstrual blockage that does not respond to numerous therapies.[107p]

This is a list of medicinal ingredients and their preparations.

  • Use one and a half taels each of lacquer, earth gourd root, arrowroot, and peony.
  • Use forty each of insects (lower insects) and larvae.
  • Use seventy each of leeches and silkworms.
  • Use two taels each of peach kernels and turtle shells.
  • Use one and a half taels each of Chinese red peony, achyranthes, yellow scutellaria, evodia, rhubarb, cinnamon heart, and bupleurum.
  • Use four qian of hemp seeds, and two pieces the size of a quail egg.
  • Use two qian of a herb (indicated by its radical).

Grind these ingredients into a powder, mix with honey to form pills, take fifteen pills the size of a walnut daily with wine, gradually increasing to thirty pills, three times a day. Continue using the leftover wine to take the previously prepared pills.

For the wine infusion, this wine is excellent for taking the aforementioned medicines.

  • Use three sheng of hemp seeds, two sheng of the herb, one sheng of peach kernels, four taels each of cinnamon heart and charcoal from the stove, six taels each of earth gourd root and arrowroot, and eight taels of achyranthes.

Macerate these ingredients in three dou of clear wine in a silk bag for five nights; or take them alone without the previous medicine.

For the treatment of menstrual obstruction and lack of appetite:

  • Use four taels of oyster, one pound of rhubarb, five pounds of bupleurum, three taels of dried ginger, two and a half taels each of ligusticum and poria, ten taels of Sichuan pepper, five qian each of coix seed, sodium sulfate, and apricot kernels, and half a tael each of leeches and silkworms, and seventy peach kernels.

Grind these thirteen ingredients into a powder, form pills the size of a walnut with honey, and take seven pills three times a day.

Shen Xiong Pill
For treating women's menstrual disorders.
Ingredients:

  • Dahuang (Rhubarb) 2 liang
  • Huangqin (Scutellaria) 2 liang
  • Qianniuzi (Plantago) 4 liang
  • Huashi (Talc) 4 liang

Grind these into a fine powder, moisten with water to form small pills the size of a mung bean. Take 10 to 15 pills with warm water, increasing by 10 pills each dose, three times a day. Cold water can also be used. It is better to use honey in the pills for added benefit. Not suitable for pregnant women or women with excessive postnatal bleeding.

Er Qi Decoction
For irregular menstruation, cessation of periods, pale complexion, thin body, loss of appetite, and internal dryness and heat, use in combination with Chai Hu Decoction.
Ingredients:

  • Dahuang 4 liang (separate for powder)
  • Vinegar 1 sheng, slow-cooked to syrup
  • Danggui (Angelica) 2 liang
  • Baishao (White Peony) 2 liang

Grind the above into powder, combine with syrup to form pills the size of a tung seed. Take 20 pills with diluted vinegar soup before meals, three times a day. If menstruation is blocked, stir-fry 9 qian of dry lacquer to release fire toxin, add 0.5 liang of myrrh and 3 qian of realgar, grind together. Also include 2 qian of Guizhi (Cinnamon Twig) and 3 qian of Panda, stir-fry until cooked; raw may cause vomiting and diarrhea.

Hu Po San: For treating women's menstrual obstruction, causing unbearable pain in the abdomen and navel, as well as common qi and blood pains, and postpartum blood rising to the heart.

"Ji Sheng" has Yan Hu and Wu Yao each one liang, without Pu Huang and Ju Hua.

Shi Mi Xiang Fu Wan: For treating irregular menstruation.

Jiawei Yangrong Wan: Treats conditions such as problems with the meridians after menstruation, inner restlessness, cough, reduced appetite, dizziness, stagnation, blood wind and qi stagnation, long-term infertility, and all symptoms from phlegm-heat that do not respond to strong tonification. Taking this can lead to pregnancy. It also treats issues related to fetal movement and leakage before pregnancy; regular use can prevent miscarriage.

Ingredients:

  • 2 liang of Angelica Sinensis (Danggui)
  • 2 liang of Prepared Rehmannia (Shudihuang)
  • 2 liang of Atractylodes (Bai Zhu)
  • 1.5 liang each of Peony (Bai Shao), Chuanxiong, Scutellaria (Huangqin), and Cyperus (Xiangfu)
  • 1 liang each of Tangerine Peel (Chenpi), Fritillaria, Poria (Fuling), and Ophiopogon (Mai Men Dong)
  • 49 peeled black beans (chao qu pi)
  • 7 qian of donkey-hide gelatin (Ejiao)
  • 5 qian of Licorice (Gancao)

Grind these into a fine powder, mix with honey to form pills the size of walnut. Take 70-80 pills with warm salt water or wine as desired. Avoid all blood-related foods.

Nü Jindan: Treats women's menstrual issues after menstruation, red or white discharge, bleeding with dripping, and long-term blood wind symptoms.

Ingredients:

  • 1 liang each of White Peony (Bai Shao), Angelica Sinensis (Danggui), Chuanxiong, Ginseng (Ren Shen), Atractylodes (Bai Zhu), Poria (Fuling), Dry Root (Gao Ben), White Angelica (Bai Zhi), White Peony, Cinnamon (Gui Xin), Corydalis (Yan Hu Suo), Peony Root (Mu Dan Pi), and Red Stone Fat (Chi Shi Zhi), all soaked in wine for three days and dried.
  • Separate grind Myrrh

Grind these into a fine powder, mix with honey to form pills the size of walnut. Take 50 pills with warm wine.[117p]

　　大乌鸡丸　治妇人羸瘦，血虚有热，经水不调，崩漏带下，不能成胎，骨蒸等证。　　四制香附一斤　熟地黄四两　生地黄　当归　白芍　黄芪　牛膝　柴胡　牡丹皮　知母　川贝母去心，各二两　黄连　地骨皮　干姜　延胡索各一两　茯苓二两半　秦艽一两半　白毛乌骨鹤一只，闭死去毛肠净　蕲艾叶　青蒿各四两，一半入鸡腹内，将鸡并余艾蒿同入坛内，以童便和水浸过二寸许，煮烂取出，去骨焙干　　右为末，用鸡汁打糊丸梧子大，服五六十丸至七八十丸，温酒或米饮下。忌煎炒苋菜。其鸡如得白丝毛乌骨崇冠者尤妙。须另于一处，以黄芪炒末为丸喂之，不可近雌鸡。如月水先期，如黄芩、黄连、地骨皮。如月水后期，如参、朮、黄芪。如白带，加二朮、香附、升麻、白芷，柴胡。如筋骨疼痛，去肉用骨。[118p]

Great Black Chicken Pill
This treats women who are weak, with blood deficiency and internal heat, irregular menstruation, excessive bleeding, vaginal discharge, inability to conceive, and symptoms like bone fever.
Ingredients:

  • Fragrant Cyperus (prepared) - 1 pound
  • Cooked Rehmannia - 4 taels
  • Raw Rehmannia - 4 taels
  • Angelica - 4 taels
  • White Peony - 4 taels
  • Astragalus - 4 taels
  • Achyranthes - 4 taels
  • Bupleurum - 4 taels
  • Peony Root - 4 taels
  • Anemarrhena - 2 taels
  • Fritillaria without heart - 2 taels
  • Coptis - 1 tael
  • Earth Bone Skin - 1 tael
  • Dried Ginger - 1 tael
  • Corydalis - 1 tael
  • Poria - 2 and a half taels
  • Gentian - 1 and a half taels
  • A black-boned, white-feathered crane - 1, with its feathers plucked and cleaned
  • Mugwort leaves - 4 taels
  • Qinghao (Sweet Wormwood) - 4 taels

Half of the herbs go inside the chicken. Place the chicken and the remaining herbs in a pot, soak with children's urine mixed with water about two inches deep, and boil until tender. Take it out, remove the bones, and dry.
Grind the mixture into a fine powder. Make pills the size of a walnut using chicken juice as binding, taking 50 to 80 pills with warm wine or rice wine. Avoid consuming fried or stir-fried amaranth. The chicken is better if it has fine white feathers and a majestic black bone.

It is essential to feed separately using powdered Astragalus to form pills, avoiding proximity to hens. For the timing of menstruation: if early, use Huangqin, Huanglian, and Earth Bone Skin. If late, use ginseng, Atractylodes, and Astragalus. For white discharge, add Atractylodes, Fragrant Cyperus, Rhizoma and Angelica, and Bupleurum. For muscle and joint pain, use only bone without flesh.[118p]

　　小乌鸡丸　治妇人经病及一切诸证。　　吴茱萸　良姜　白姜　当归　芍药　延胡索　破故纸　川椒　陈皮　青皮　刘寄奴　川芎　生地黄　莪朮各一两　荷叶灰四两　北艾二两　　右为末，用乌骨鸡一只，取肉煮烂，和为丸梧子大，每服五十丸。如月水不通，苏木红花酒下。如腹痛血色黑者，加炒黄连。如有痰湿者，加南星、苍朮、香附。如未曾生育过者，门户油膜包裹子宫，因此不孕，宜加凤凰衣七个，烧存性，朱砂为衣。[119p]

Little Black Chicken Pills treat women's menstrual disorders and various other symptoms.

Ingredients:

  • Wu Zhu Yu (Evodia fruit)
  • Liang Jiang (dried ginger)
  • Bai Jiang (white ginger)
  • Dang Gui (Angelica sinensis)

  • Qing Pi (green tangerine peel)

  • Bei Ai (mugwort) – two liang.

These ingredients are powdered. Take one black-boned chicken, boil the meat until tender, and mix to form pills the size of a date. Each dose is fifty pills.

If there is menstrual obstruction, take with Su Mu (Sandalwood) and Hong Hua (Safflower) wine. For abdominal pain with dark blood, add fried Huang Lian (Coptis). If there is phlegm and dampness, add Nan Xing (Arisaema) and Cang Zhu (Atractylodes) and Xiang Fu (Cyperus).

For women who have never given birth and are infertile due to oil film covering the uterus, add seven pieces of Phoenix feather, burned for residual essence, and cover with cinnabar.[119p]

如胎不安，蜜酒下。如血崩，豆淋酒调棉灰下。如肠风，陈米饮调百草霜下。如心疼，菖蒲酒下。如漏胎下血，乌梅酒下。如死胎不下，螌蝥三个煎酒下。如腰脚痛，当归酒下。如头风，薄荷煎汤下。如血气眼黑，甘草煎汤下。如生疮，地黄煎汤下。如身体疼痛，黄芪末调酒下。如胎前产后白痢，干姜煎汤下；赤痢，甘草煎汤下。如气块血块作痛，与葱白汤间服。如子宫久冷，茯苓煎汤下。如赤带，茶清下。如耳聋，腊茶清下。其余百病，酢汤下。[120p]

If the fetus is unstable, administer honey wine. If there is excessive bleeding, use a mixture of mung bean and wine with cotton ash. For intestinal wind, use aged rice wine mixed with various herbs. For heart pain, use calamus wine. If there is leakage of blood from a miscarriage, administer black plum wine. If there is a retained dead fetus, use three boiled locusts mixed with wine. For pain in the waist and legs, use angelica wine. For headaches, administer mint decoction. If there are darkened eyes due to blood stagnation, use licorice decoction. For sores, use rehmannia decoction. For body aches, mix Astragalus powder with wine. For white diarrhea before or after childbirth, use dried ginger decoction; for red diarrhea, use licorice decoction. For painful lumps of qi and blood, alternate with scallion white soup. If the uterus has been cold for a long time, administer poria decoction. For red discharge, use clear tea. For deafness, use wax tea. For remaining ailments, use vinegar soup.[120p]

Bao Dan Wan
Treats the impending menstrual flow of young women, preventing the accumulation of startled evil; also treats all forms of surprise, terror, and mania in men and women, showing miraculous results.

  • 1.5 taels of black lead
  • 2 taels of mercury
  • 1 tael each of cinnabar and乳香 (frankincense)

First, melt the black lead in a basin; then add the mercury, waiting until it forms into grains. Next, add the cinnabar and frankincense powder. While hot, mix well using a willow branch pestle, forming pills the size of a lotus seed. Each pill is to be swallowed with clear well water on an empty stomach. The patient should be allowed to sleep without disturbance; waking induces calm. A second pill may eliminate the root cause.

Furthmore, form honey pills the size of walnuts, taking 60 to 70 pills with clear tea.[121p]

Wan Ying Wan: Treats worms, menstrual disorders, and abdominal pain.

妇人经脉门

　　益气养荣汤 【《医案》】　治经事久不调，变成瘵疾。　　白朮炒，二钱　人参　茯苓　陈皮　贝母　香附　当归酒拌　川芎　黄芪盐水拌炒　熟地蒸　芍药炒，各一钱　甘草炙　桔梗各五分　　右，姜水煎服。

　　杏林摘要方 【《本草》】　治子宫虚寒，下元虚，月水不调，或闭或漏，或崩中带下，或产后败血未尽，内结不散，无子。　　红娘子六十枚　大黄　皂荚　葶苈各一两　巴豆一百二十枚　　右为末，枣肉为丸弹子大，以绵裹留系，用竹筒送入阴户，一时许发热，渴用熟汤一二盏解之，后发寒静睡，要安三日，方取出。每日空心以鸡子三枚、胡椒末二分炒食酒下以补之，久则子宫暖矣。[123p]

Ziweisan
Treats women with menstrual flow issues, symptoms of heat and abdominal distension.
Ingredients: Ziwei, cassia, red peony root, yan husi, bai zhi, angelica, peony bark, Liu Jin's herb in equal parts, with a small amount of red flower.
Preparation: Use one cup of wine, two cups of water, and decoct for consumption.

Benefits of Qi and Nourishing Decoction
Treats prolonged menstrual disorders that have transformed into tuberculosis-like conditions.
Ingredients: Stir-fried white atra (bai zhu) 2 qian, ginseng, poria, aged tangerine peel, fritillaria, cyperus, angelica mixed with wine, chuan xiong, astragalus mixed with salt, steamed cooked earth (shu di), stir-fried peony root, each 1 qian; honey-fried licorice, and balloon flower each 5 fen.
Preparation: Decoct with ginger water for consumption.

Summary of the Apricot Forest Prescription
Treats uterine coldness, lower source deficiency, menstrual irregularities, vaginal leakage, mid-cycle bleeding, or residual postpartum blood, internal issues preventing conception.
Ingredients: 60 pieces of red lady (hong niang zi), 1 liang of rhubarb, soap pod, and tergum-leaf, each 1 liang; 120 pieces of castor bean.
Preparation: Grind into powder, make into pill-sized balls with jujube flesh, wrapped in cotton, inserted into the vagina for a while until warmth is felt. If thirsty, use 1-2 cups of cooked broth to alleviate it. Afterward, if cold, rest for three days before removal. Each morning on an empty stomach, consume 3 eggs and 2 fen of pepper powder sautéed with wine for nourishment. After a while, the uterus will be warmed.[123p]

　　补中汤 【东垣】　治经行冒寒，用此加表药。　　升麻　柴胡各二钱　当归身二分　泽泻四分　五味子二十一粒　炙甘草八分　黄芪二钱半　神曲三分　红花少许　大麦糵五分　　右作二服，水煎，食前服。

　　紫金丸 【《产乳》】　治久有瘀血，月水不调，黄瘦不食，亦治产后恶露不快，腰腹痛，寒热头痛。　　五灵脂水淘净炒末，一两　真蒲黄末分两未开　　右以好米酢调稀，慢火熬膏，入真蒲黄末、五灵脂未，和丸龙眼大，每服一丸，以水与童子小便各半盏，煎至七分，温服，少顷再服，恶露即下。血块经闭者，酒磨服之。[124p]

Buzhong Decoction (by Dongyuan)
For treating menstrual issues combined with cold, use this with exterior medicines.

  • Shengma (Radix Cimicifugae) 6g
  • Chaihu (Radix Bupleuri) 6g
  • Danggui (Radix Angelicae Sinensis) 4g
  • Zexie (Rhizoma Alismatis) 16g
  • Wuwuzi (Fructus Schisandrae) 21 grains
  • Zhi Gancao (Honey-Fried Licorice Root) 6g
  • Huangqi (Radix Astragali) 12.5g
  • Shenqu (Fermented Mass) 3g
  • Honghua (Flos Carthami) a little
  • Damaizi (Barley Ferment) 5g
    Prepare 2 doses, decoct in water, and take before meals.

Zijin Pill (from "Chanyi")
For treating prolonged stagnant blood, irregular menstrual flow, yellowish and thin body lacking appetite, also for postpartum lingering discharge, lower abdomen pain, and cold or hot headaches.

  • Wulingzhi (Resina Laccae) cleaned and roasted finely, 37.5g
  • Zhenpuhuang (True Pollen) divided into two parts, not opened
    Mix and use good rice vinegar to dilute, slowly cook into a paste, then add True Pollen and Wulingzhi, mix into pills the size of longan.
    Take one pill, mix with half a cup of water and half a cup of young boy’s urine, decoct until 70% remains, drink warm, and take again after a while; the discharge will descend. For blood clots causing missed periods, take with wine.[124p]

　　乌鸦散 【《本草》，下同】　治经脉不通。　　乌鸦去皮毛炙，三分　当归焙　好墨各三分　延胡索炒　蒲黄炒　水蛭以糯米炒过，各半两　芫青以糯米炒过，一分　　右为末，每服一钱，酒下。

　　獭胆丸　治月水不通。
　　干獭胆一枚　水蛭炒黄，十枚　干狗胆　硇砂　川椒炒去汗并目，各一分　　右为末，酢糊丸菉豆大，每服五丸，当归酒下，日一。
　　经验方　妇人五十后经水不止者，作败血论，用此方；亦治女子经闭。　　小儿胎发一枚，烧存性　生地　茜根各一两　阿胶　侧柏叶　炒黄芩各五钱　　右分六贴，每贴水一盏半，煎七分，入胎发灰服之。[125p]

Crow Scattering
Treats obstructed meridians.
Remove the skin and fur from the crow and roast it. Take three parts each of processed Angelica, good ink, fried Corydalis, and fried Bulrush pollen, along with half an ounce each of processed leeches, and one part of processed blue-green herbs. Grind these into a powder. Take one qian (a weight unit) with wine.

Otter Gallbladder Pill
Treats menstrual stoppage.
One dried otter gallbladder, ten fried leeches until yellow, one dried dog gallbladder, one part of realgar, one part of Sichuan pepper (fried to remove sweat and vision), all equal in quantity. Grind these into a powder and mix with vinegar to form pills the size of mung beans. Take five pills each time with Angelica wine, once daily.
Proven Formula
For women over fifty with prolonged menstrual bleeding, use this formula, also treats women with menstrual disorders.
One piece of fetal hair, burnt to preserve its properties; one pound each of raw Rehmannia and madder root; and five qian each of donkey-hide gelatin and toasted Arborvitae leaves; and fried Scutellaria. Divide into six doses. Each dose uses one and a half cups of water, decocted to seven-tenths, then take it with fetal hair ash.[125p]

　　玉烛散 【《治法汇》】　治二便闭塞，月事不行。　　四物汤　芒硝　大黄　甘草各味，分两随宜　　右，姜三片，煎服。

　　四物加黄芩黄连汤海藏　治经水如黑豆汁。　　四物汤四两　黄芩　黄连各一两
　　右为末，酢糊丸服。

　　卫生汤 【《准绳》，下同】　血枯经闭，服芩连、三和、玉烛之后，宜服此汤。　　当归　白芍药各二两　黄芪三两　甘草一两　　右为末，每服半两，水二盏，煎至一盏，空心温服。如虚加人参一两。
　　万病丸　一名万痛丸。治经事不来，绕脐痛。　　干漆杵碎炒烟尽　牛膝酒浸一宿焙干，各一两　　右为末，以生地黄汁一升，入二味药末，银器内慢火熬可丸，即丸如桐子大，每服二十丸，空心，米饮或温酒下。
　　四物加葵花汤　治经水濇少。[126p]

Jade Candle Dispersion 【“Law Collection”】
For treating obstruction of two passages and irregular menstrual flow.
Four Substance Decoction, each ingredient: Mangxiao, Dahuang, and Gancao, in proportion as needed.
Additionally, three slices of ginger, decoct and take.

Four Substance Decoction with Huangqin and Huanglian for treating menstrual flow that resembles black bean juice.
Four Substance Decoction, four ounces; Huangqin and Huanglian, each one ounce.
Grind these into powder, mix with vinegar to form pills for consumption.

Health Preservation Decoction 【“Standard Reference”, same below】
For blood depletion and menstrual closure, after taking Huangqin, Huanglian, and Jade Candle, it is advisable to take this decoction.
Each of the following: Danggui and Baishao, two ounces each; Huangqi, three ounces; Gancao, one ounce.
Grind into powder; for each dose, take half an ounce, boil with two cups of water until reduced to one cup, and consume warm on an empty stomach. If weak, add one ounce of Renshen.

Wanbing Wan, also known as Wan Tong Wan. For treating lack of menstrual flow and pain around the navel.
Crushed and roasted qiqi until smoke dissipates; Niuxi soaked in wine overnight and dried, each one ounce.
Grind these into powder, mix with one liter of raw Dihuang juice, slow-cook in a silver pot until elements can be formed into pills, each the size of a tung seed. Take twenty pills each time, on an empty stomach, with rice drink or warm wine.

Four Substance Decoction with Sunflower for treating scanty menstrual flow.[126p]

Four Substance Decoction: four taels; Sunflower: one tael.
Prepare five or four doses with water and take as a decoction. One formula adds safflower for irregular menstruation.

Four Substance Decoction with Cooked Rehmannia and Angelica:
Used for scanty menstrual flow with normal color. Ingredients: Four Substance Decoction: four taels; Cooked Rehmannia and Angelica: each one tael. Prepare five or four doses with water and take as a decoction.

Xianqi Decoction: used for early menstruation, suitable for cooling blood and stabilizing menstruation.
Ingredients: Fresh Rehmannia, Wild Angelica, White Peony: each two qian; Huangbo, Zhimu: each one qian; Mugwort, Xiangfu, Roasted Licorice: each seven fen; Baizhi, Huanglian, Chuanxiong, and fried Ejiao: each eight fen. Prepare with two sheng of water, decoct to one sheng, and take warm before meals.

Tugua Root Powder (from "Jinkui"): Used for irregular menstruation and lower abdominal fullness and pain, especially if it reappears after a month.
Ingredients: Tugua root, Peony, Cinnamon Twig: each seven and a half qian. Grind these four ingredients into a powder, take a thumb-sized amount with wine three times a day.

Overdue Decoction (from "Standards", and similarly below): Used for menstruation that is overdue, caused by blood deficiency and qi stagnation; the method should nourish blood and move qi.
Ingredients: Cooked Rehmannia, White Peony, Angelica, Xiangfu (vinegar-prepared): each two qian; Chuanxiong: one qian; Safflower: seven qian; Peach Kernel paste: six fen; Poria, Mutong: each five fen; Licorice, Cinnamon: each four fen. Prepare with two sheng of water, decoct to one sheng, and take warm before meals.[127p]

Ziyue Decoction is used to treat women with deficiency in heart and lung, weak blood vessels, and delayed menstruation. The ingredients are: ginseng, yam, and astragalus, each 3 grams; white poria peeled, ligusticum, angelica, white peony, and cooked rehmannia, each 4.5 grams. Prepare one dose with two cups of water, boil down to one cup, and take before meals.

Ginseng Blood Nourishing Pills are for women with inherent weakness, deficient blood and qi. Regular use tonifies the Chong and Ren channels, regulates menstruation, and warms the lower abdomen, generating blood and qi. The ingredients are: three taels of black plum flesh, five taels of cooked rehmannia, two taels of angelica, and one tael each of ginseng, ligusticum, red peony, and roasted cattail pollen. Grind into a fine powder, mix with honey to form pills the size of walnuts, with a dosage of eighty pills taken with warm rice wine or drink.

Harmonizing Xiaoyao Powder treats blood deficiency with heat, menstrual irregularities, abdominal pain, and phlegm cough with tidal heat. The ingredients are: one tael each of angelica, white atractylodes, white peony, bupleurum, and poria; half tael of roasted licorice. Grind and take half a tael each time, decocted with ginger and mint leaves. If lacking angelica, peony, and licorice, substitute with equal parts ginseng and astragalus.

Zengsun Siwu Decoction is for menstrual irregularities, abdominal pain, to nourish blood, and warm the vessels. The ingredients are: one and a half grams of ligusticum, angelica, white peony, cooked rehmannia, and peony bark; one gram of earth bone bark. Prepare one dose with two cups of water, boil down to one cup, and take before meals.[128p]

Chenxiang Jiangqi San: Calms the qi, regulates the pathway, and unblocks the blood vessels. Ingredients such as Wuye, Muxiang, Xiangfuzi, Sharen, and Gancao are each measured in equal parts. Grind them into a fine powder, and take two qian mixed with warm salt water on an empty stomach.

Yeqi San (from "Jisheng"): Treats conditions in women where qi is excessive compared to blood, resulting in various symptoms such as head pressure and chest fullness. Ingredients: four liang Xiangfu, one qian Fuzhen, one qian Gancao (roasted), and two liang Chenpi. Grind into a powder, and take two qian mixed with boiling water before meals.

Zhengqi Tianxiang Tang (from "Ganzhu"): Treats all qi-related conditions in women, where qi ascends and affects the heart, causing pressure in the chest and stabbing pain in the sides, and menstrual disturbances. Ingredients: two qian Tai Wuye, eight qian Xiangfu, one liang Chenpi, one liang Suye, and five fen dried ginger. Chew them, and take seven to eight qian decocted in water.

Danggui Yin (from "Zhunsong"): Suppresses yang and aids yin, regulates the meridians. Ingredients include lightly roasted Danggui, steamed and baked Shengdi, Chuanxiong, Baizhu, Baishaoyao, and Huangqin in equal parts. Take three qian with one and a half cups of water, simmer until reduced to eight-tenths, and take warm on an empty stomach.

Qifei Tang: Treats deficiencies of Ying and Wei, irregular menstruation, whether excessive or insufficient, and abdominal pain. Ingredients: Danggui, Chuanxiong, Baishaoyao, Póngzhú, Shudi, Chuanjiang, and Muxiang in equal parts. Take four qian with one and a half cups of water, simmer until reduced to eight-tenths, and take warm. Additionally, a formula from Danxi treats excessive menstrual flow.[129p]

Huangqin wine fried, Baishaoyao wine fried, and turtle shell crisp roasted, each one tael; Chunzhu root bark seven and a half qian; Huangba fried, three qian; Xiangfu two and a half qian. The above should be ground into powder, mixed with wine to make pills, taken with a light white broth, five to sixty pills.

Yiwai Shengyang Decoction treats women's irregular menstruation, or weakness in the pulse and reduced appetite after blood loss, watery diarrhea, occurring two to three times a day. Huangqi two qian, Baizhu three qian, fried Qu 1.5 qian, Danggui, Chenpi, roasted licorice, and Ren Shen each one qian; Shengma, Huangqin, and Chaihu each half a qian. The above should be ground (in mouth), take half a tael each time, decocted with water. Remove Huangqin in autumn. If there is abdominal pain, add Shaoyao; if there is a cough, remove Ren Shen.

Da Wenjing Decoction [from "Jinkui"] treats deficiency of Chong and Ren, menstrual irregularities, or excessive menstrual flow, or delay in menstruation, or excessive bleeding during menstruation, or complications from pregnancy, blood stasis, severe pain in the lower abdomen, and disturbance of the five hearts with heat. Wu Zhuyu decoction with Paeonia bark, Bai Shaoyao, cinnamon without coarse skin, Ren Shen, Danggui, Chuanxiong, stir-fried Ejiao, and roasted licorice, each one qian; Maimendong without the seed, two qian; Banxia two and a half qian. This should be made into one dose, using two sheng of water, five slices of fresh ginger, and decocted until one sheng remains, to be taken before meals.[130p]

Xiao Wenjing Decoction (from "Simple Formulas")
For treating irregularities in the menstrual cycle and cold pain in the blood organs.
Ingredients: equal parts of Angelica sinensis and prepared Aconite.
Instructions: Slice and take three qian, boil with one cup of water until reduced to eight parts, and take warm on an empty stomach.

Wenjing Decoction (from "Harmonious Formulas")
For treating women's deficiency of blood and coldness in the blood sea, resulting in irregular menstrual flow.
Ingredients: 1.5 qian each of Chuanxiong, Angelica sinensis, Peony, and Atractylodes; 2 qian each of Ginseng and Achyranthes; 1 qian each of Cinnamon and Moutan; 0.5 qian of Licorice.
Instructions: Boil with two cups of water until reduced to one cup, and take at any time.

Zi Xue Decoction (from "Standards," as below)
For nourishing the blood, benefiting women, and treating prolonged cold in the blood sea.
Ingredients: 1.5 qian of Angelica sinensis; 1.5 qian each of Chuanxiong, Ophiopogon (remove the heart), Moutan, Ginseng, Peony, and Amber (ground separately); 0.5 qian each of Banxia, Cinnamon, fried Ejiao, sour jujube seed, and Licorice.
Instructions: Prepare as one dose, boil with two cups of water and three slices of ginger until reduced to one cup, and take before meals.[131p]

　　加味吴茱萸汤　治冲任衰弱，月候愆期，或前或后，或崩漏不止，赤白带下，小腹急痛，每至经脉行时，头眩，饮食或少，气满心怯，肌肉不泽，悉皆治之。　　半夏二钱　吴茱萸　当归各一钱半　麦门冬　干姜　白茯苓　桔梗　南木香　防风　丹皮　甘草各一钱　官桂　北细辛各五分　　右作一服，水二锺，生姜三片，煎至一锺，食前服。
　　桃仁散　治妇人月水不调，或淋沥不断，断后复来，状如泻水，四体虚倦，不能饮食，腹中坚痛，不可行动，月水或前或后，或经月不来，多思酸物。　　桃仁　半夏　当归　川牛膝　桂心　人参　蒲黄　丹皮　川芎　泽兰叶各一钱　赤芍药　生地黄各一钱半　粉草五分　　右作一服，水二锺，姜三片，红枣一枚，煎至一锺，食前服。[132p]

Jiawei Wuzhuyu Decoction is used to treat weakened Chong and Ren channels, irregular menstrual cycles—either earlier or later than expected—or continuous bleeding, discharge that is red or white, sharp pain in the lower abdomen that occurs with the menstrual flow, dizziness, decreased appetite, a sense of fullness and fearfulness, and lack of luster in the flesh. All of these conditions can be treated with this remedy. The ingredients include:

  • 2 qian of Banxia,
  • 1.5 qian each of Wuzhuyu, Danggui,
  • 1 qian each of Maidong, Ganjiang, Baifuling, Jiegeng, Nankuxiang, Fangfeng, Danpi, and Gancao,
  • 0.5 qian each of Guangkui and Beixixin.

Prepare it by boiling with 2 sheng of water, 3 slices of fresh ginger, until reduced to 1 sheng, and take it before meals.

Taoren Powder is used to treat women's menstrual irregularities, persistent dripping, recurrences, resembling watery discharge, feelings of great weakness and fatigue, inability to eat, hard pain in the abdomen preventing movement, irregular menstrual cycles, or absence of menstruation for long periods, with cravings for sour foods. The ingredients include:

  • 1 qian each of Taoren, Banxia, Danggui, Chuanniuxi, Guixin, Renshen, Puhuang, Danpi, Chuanqiang, and Zexianye,
  • 1.5 qian each of Chishao and Shengdihuang,
  • 0.5 qian of Fencao.

Prepare it by boiling with 2 sheng of water, 3 slices of ginger, and 1 red date until reduced to 1 sheng, and take it before meals.[132p]

　　姜黄散　治血脏久冷，月水不调，脐腹刺痛。　　片子姜黄　白芍药各二钱　延胡索　牡丹皮　当归各钱半　蓬朮　红花　桂心　川芎各一钱　　右作一服，水二锺，酒半锺，煎至一锺，不拘时服。
　　紫石英丸 【《本事方》】　治妇人月经乍多乍少，或前或后，时发疼痛。　　紫石英细研水飞　川乌炮　杜仲炒去丝　禹余粮煅酢淬　远志去心　泽泻　桑寄生　桂心　龙骨别研　当归　人参　肉苁蓉酒浸　石斛　干姜炮　五味子　甘草炙，各一两　牡蛎煅　川椒去目并合口者不用，炒出汗，各半两　　右为细末，炼蜜和九如梧子大，每服二十丸，食前用米饮汤下。

Turmeric Powder: Treats long-standing cold in the blood vessels, menstrual irregularities, and sharp pain in the abdomen. Use: 2 qian of turmeric and white peony, 1/2 qian each of Corydalis, peony root, and angelica, 1 qian each of agrimony, safflower, cinnamon heart, and chuanxiong. Combine these into one dose, use 2 sheng of water and 1/2 sheng of wine, and decoct until reduced to 1 sheng. Take at any time.

Amethyst Pill [from "Benshi Fang"]: Treats women's menstrual irregularities, with variations in flow and timing, accompanied by pain. Ingredients: finely ground amethyst, processed chuan wu, roasted du zhong (removing fibers), calcined yu yu liang, removing hearts from yuan zhi, ze xie, sang ji sheng, cinnamon heart, separately ground dragon bone, angelica, ginseng, alcohol-soaked cistanche, dendrobium, processed dry ginger, schisandra, and honey-roasted licorice, each 1 liang. For oyster, calcined, and chuan jiao (removing seeds and not using those stuck together), use 1/2 liang each, fry until sweat comes out. Combine into a fine powder, mix with honey to form pills the size of walnut. Take 20 pills before meals with rice soup.

Warming the Womb Pill [from "Zhunsheng", same applies]: Treats deficiency of the Chong and Ren channels, prolonged cold in the lower jiao, menstrual irregularities, infertility, abnormal bleeding, and both red and white discharge. Ingredients: 6 liang of raw sulfur, fire-calcined red stone resin, processed fu zi (removing skin and navel), three liang each of hai piao xiao. For yu yu liang, fire-calcine and process, 9 liang total. Combine into a fine powder, form pills the size of phoenix seeds with vinegar paste. Take 30 pills on an empty stomach with warm wine or vinegar soup.[133p]

　　内补当归丸　治血气虚损，月水不调，或崩中漏下，去血过多，肌体羸困，及月水将行，腰腿重痛。　　当归去芦炒　阿胶炒　白芷　续断　干姜炮　芎藭　甘草炙，各四两　熟地黄半两焙　芍药　附子炮去皮脐　肉桂各二两　吴茱萸汤泡，焙　白朮各三两　蒲黄八钱，炒　　右为细末，炼蜜和丸如梧桐子大，每服五十丸，空心用温酒送下。

Nei Bu Dang Gui Wan: Treats blood and qi deficiency, menstrual irregularities, or excessive bleeding during menstruation, fatigue of the body, and heavy pain in the waist and legs before menstruation. Ingredients: Dang Gui (Angelica sinensis) without the root, roasted; Ejiao (donkey-hide gelatin) roasted; Bai Zhi (Angelica dahurica); Xu Duan (Dipsacus asperoides); Gan Jiang (dried ginger) processed; Chuan Xiong (Ligusticum chuanxiong); Gan Cao (licorice) roasted, each four taels; Shu Di Huang (cooked rehmannia) half a tael, roasted; Shao Yao (Paeonia lactiflora); Fu Zi (Aconitum carmichaelii) processed and peeled; Rou Gui (cinnamon) each two taels; Wu Zhu Yu (Evodia rutaecarpa) soaked in decoction, roasted; Bai Zhu (Atractylodes macrocephala) each three taels; Pu Huang (catkins of Typha angustifolia) eight qian, roasted. Grind all into a fine powder, refine with honey, and form into pills the size of Wutong seeds. Take fifty pills each time, consumed with warm wine on an empty stomach.

Yu Yu Liang Wan: Treats blood deficiency and heat, menstrual irregularities, red and white leucorrhea, gradually leading to excessive bleeding. Ingredients: Yu Yu Liang (a specific mineral) calcined and refined; Bai Shi Zhi (bamboo fat), each one tael; Sang Ji Sheng (Mulberry Misteltoe); Fu Zi (Aconitum carmichaelii) processed and peeled; Bie Jia (soft-shelled turtle shell) without the skirt, calcined; Dang Gui; Bai Zhu; Hou Po (Magnolia officinalis) with rough skin removed; Bai Ye (cypress leaves) roasted, each one tael; Shao Yao (Paeonia lactiflora); Gou Ji (Cibotium barometz) peeled, each seven and a half qian; Wu Zhu Yu (Evodia rutaecarpa) soaked in decoction, roasted, half a tael. 　　鹿茸丸　治冲任虚损，又为风寒所乘，尺脉微小，甚者可灸关元穴。　　鹿耳炙　赤石脂　禹余粮各一两　续断二两　柏叶炒　附子炮去皮脐　熟地黄　当归酒浸　艾叶各七钱半　　右为末，酒糊丸梧子大，每股五十丸，空心温酒下。

Jiao Jia Powder: Treats disharmony of the protective and nutritive qi, menstrual blood stasis, and alleviates abdominal pain from menstrual issues.
Ingredients: Extract juice from fresh ginger, set aside the residue; 2 jin of fresh rehmannia, extract juice and set aside the residue; 1 tael each of white peony, angelica, and cassia heart, ½ tael each of myrrh (ground) and fried safflower; 1 tael of yanhusuo (prepared by steaming and removing the skin) and 1 tael of cattail pollen (fried separated by paper). 　　交加地黄丸　治妇人经不调，血块气痞，肚腹疼痛。　　生地黄捣汁存滓　老生姜捣汁存滓，各一斤　延胡索　当归　川芎　芍药各二两　没药　木香各一两　桃仁去皮尖研　人参各半两　香附半斤　　右为末，先以生姜汁浸地黄滓，以地黄汁浸生姜滓，晒干，皆以汁尽为度，共十一味，作一处晒干，研为末，酢糊为丸，空心，以姜汤下。
　　交加散　治妇人荣卫不通，经脉不调，腹中撮痛，气多血少，结聚为症，产后中风。　　生地黄　生姜各五两，各研取汁
　　右，交互取汁浸一夕，各炒黄，渍汁尽为度，末之。如寻常腹痛，酒调下三钱。如产后，尤不可缺。[139p]

Jiao Jia Di Huang Wan treats women with irregular menstruation, blood clots and qi stagnation, as well as abdominal pain.

Ingredients:

  • Fresh Rehmannia root (sheng di huang) juice with residue, 1 pound
  • Fresh ginger juice with residue, 1 pound
  • Corydalis tuber (yan hu suo), 2 taels
  • Angelica sinensis (dang gui), 2 taels
  • Ligusticum chuanxiong (chuan xiong), 2 taels
  • White peony root (bai shao), 2 taels
  • Myrrh (mo yao), 1 tael
  • Wood aromatic (mu xiang), 1 tael
  • Peach kernel (tao ren) peeled and ground, ½ tael
  • Ginseng (ren shen), ½ tael
  • Cyperus (Xiang fu), ½ pound

Prepare the powder: First, soak the Rehmannia residue in ginger juice, and the ginger residue in Rehmannia juice, then dry in sunlight until the juices are fully absorbed. Combine all eleven ingredients, dry together, pulverize into a fine powder, form into hollow pills, and take with ginger soup.

Jiao Jia San is used to address women's channel blockages, irregular circulation, abdominal cramping, excess qi, and insufficient blood, resulting in symptoms like postpartum stroke.

Ingredients:

  • Fresh Rehmannia root (sheng di huang), 5 taels
  • Fresh ginger (sheng jiang), 5 taels

Prepare by extracting juices, soaking overnight, then frying until yellow, drying completely, and pulverizing. When treating ordinary abdominal pain, take 3 qian mixed with rice wine. For postpartum care, it is especially essential.[139p]

　　桂技桃仁汤　治经候前腹痛不可忍。　　桂枝　芍药　生地黄各二两　桃仁四十枚　甘草一两　　右为粗末，每服五钱，水二盏，姜三片，枣一枚，同煎去滓温服。

Cinnamon and Peach Kernel Decoction: For treating unbearable abdominal pain before menstruation. Ingredients: Two liang each of cinnamon twig, peony root, and raw rehmannia; forty peach kernels; one liang of licorice. Grind into a coarse powder. For each dose, take five qian, boil with two cups of water, three slices of ginger, and one date. Strain and take warm.

Yan Hu Suo Decoction: For women, particularly virgin women, who suffer from emotional disturbances causing both blood and qi to mingle, leading to pain in the chest and abdomen, which may extend to the waist and sides, or cause stabbing pain in the upper and lower back, particularly when menstruation is irregular. This can address all blood and qi related pains. Ingredients: Half a liang each of processed angelica root soaked in wine and dried, fried yan hu suo (with the skin removed), fried cattail pollen, red peony root, and undehydrated cinnamon; three qian each of ginger, frankincense, myrrh, and undehydrated patchouli; and two and a half qian of fried licorice. Grind together. For each dose, take four qian, boil with one and a half cups of water, seven slices of fresh ginger, and boil until down to seven tenths. Strain and take warm before meals. If there are symptoms of nausea, add half a liang each of pinellia and tangerine peel.

Zhu Fu Wan (Cooked Attached Pill): Also known as Xiangfu Wan or Cu Fu Wan. It treats stagnant qi and menstrual irregularities, abdominal pain, sallow complexion, reduced appetite, or abnormal uterine bleeding and leucorrhea. Scrape off the hair from Xiangfuzi, boil in vinegar for half a day, then grind into a powder. Form into pills the size of walnuts; take five to seventy pills with rice wine or light vinegar soup.

Mo Fu Wan (Black Attached Pill): Treats women's menstrual irregularities and long-term infertility. Use one pound of Xiangfuzi, four taels of pure cooked Ai Ye, and one bowl of vinegar; boil until dry, then pound in a stone mortar, forming into cakes to dry on new tiles. Add one tael each of Bai Fuling, Dang Gui, Ren Shen, Chuan Xiong, and 熟地 Huang, and one tael of Jingmo baked in red vine vinegar; also five qian of Mu Xiang. Combine into a powder, mix with vinegar to form pills the size of walnuts, and take seventy to eighty pills with warm wine.

Si Zhi Xiang Fu Wan (Four Preparations of Xiangfu Pill): Treats menstrual irregularities and can harmonize the channels. Use one pound of Xiangfuzi, divided into four preparations: one soaked and cooked with saltwater and ginger juice to reduce phlegm; one cooked and lightly fried with rice vinegar to nourish the blood; one stir-fried with four taels of Zhi Zi to disperse stagnation; one washed with children's urine without frying to reduce fire. Use two taels each of Chuan Xiong and Dang Gui. Combine into a powder, mix with wine to form pills the size of walnuts, taking fifty to seventy pills, using soup according to symptoms. Add Four Gentlemen for qi deficiency, and Four Substances for blood deficiency.[147p]

　　七制香附丸 【《入门》】 　治月候不调，结成症瘕，或骨蒸发热。　　香附米十四两，分七包；一包同当归二两，酒浸；二包同蓬朮二两，童便浸；三包同牡丹皮、艾叶各一两，米泔浸；四包同乌药二两，米泔浸；五包同川芎、延胡索各一两，水浸；六包同三棱、柴胡各一两，酢浸；七包同红花、乌梅各一两，盐水浸　　右，各浸春五、夏三、秋七、冬十日，晒干，袛取香附为末，以浸药水打糊，和丸梧子大，临卧酒下八十丸。

Seven-Ingredient Xiangfu Pill

This formula treats irregular menstrual cycles, the formation of masses, or bone steaming heat.

Take 14 taels of Xiangfu (Cyperus), divided into seven packets:

  1. One packet soaked with 2 taels of Danggui in wine.
  2. Two packets soaked with 2 taels of Pungzhu in child’s urine.
  3. Three packets soaked with 1 tael each of Mudanpi and Aiye in rice wash.
  4. Four packets soaked with 2 taels of Wuyao in rice wash.
  5. Five packets soaked with 1 tael each of Chuanxiong and Yanhusuo in water.
  6. Six packets soaked with 1 tael each of Sanleng and Chaihu in vinegar.
  7. Seven packets soaked with 1 tael each of Honghua and Wumei in saltwater.

Soak each packet for 5 days in spring, 3 days in summer, 7 days in autumn, and 10 days in winter, then dry them in the sun. Take only the powdered Xiangfu, mix it with the soaking liquid to form a paste, and shape it into pills the size of walnuts. Take 80 pills with wine at bedtime.

Daojing Pill

This formula treats obstructions in the menstrual cycle and pain in the waist and abdomen.

Use:

  • 2 taels of Dahuang,
  • 1 tael each of Danggui, Chuanxiong, Baishao, Guangkui, Taoren, and Gancao,
  • 2.5 qian of Xuejie,
  • 1 qian of Honghua,
  • 20 pieces of Panmao glutinous rice, stir-fried.

Grind these into a powder, mix with honey to form pills the size of walnuts. Take 30 pills with wine. Another version includes 21 pieces of Chuanxiong and Jiji, without GanCao or Panmao.[148p]

　　乌药汤 【《东垣十书》】 　治妇人血海疼痛。　　香附子二钱　乌药一钱半　当归一钱　木香　甘草各五分　　右剉，水煎服。

Wuyao Decoction [from "Dongyuan's Ten Books"]
Treats women's dysmenorrhea.

  1. 2 qian of Xiangfuzi,
  2. 1.5 qian of Wuyao,
  3. 1 qian of Danggui,
  4. 5 fen each of Muxiang and Gancao.
    Chop the ingredients and decoct in water for consumption.

Wuji Pill [from "Ancient and Modern Medical Mirror"]
Treats amenorrhea with blood clots and severe pain.
4 liang of Jinhua Dahuang; boil 1 liang in wine, 1 liang in vinegar, 1 liang in children's urine, and 1 liang in salt water, each seven times. Combine and steam-sun-dry for another seven times.
Grind into powder, using 1.5 liang of Danggui and Shudi Huang, simmer with concentrated juice until thick, form into pills the size of a jujube, and take thirty pills with Honghua decoction.

Lixiao Powder [from "Ji Yin"]
Treats long-standing blood accumulation, persistent abdominal pain, and irregular menstruation.
Qingpi, Chenpi, Wuyiao, Ganjiang, Xiangfuzi, Pengajia, and Sanleng in equal parts.
Grind, vinegar-cook, and dry to powder, take on an empty stomach, and drink 2 qian mixed with Chenpi decoction.

Another method: take 3 sheng of raw Dihuang juice, boil down to 2 sheng and consume.

Another formula: Burn white dog feces to a powder consistency, take a small amount with wine, three times a day.
Another formula: Take one liter of white horse urine, it is beneficial.

For menstrual blockage: Take one liter of smartweed and grind it into powder, make it into honey pills the size of a bullet, wrap them in cotton and insert them three inches deep into the vagina, change each pill overnight, it induces sweating and relief.

Monthly Blood Stagnation: Cut the rhizome of the water lily finely, boil it in water, take two sheng (liters), mix with empty wine and drink.

Another Prescription: Three taels of tiger bone, one tael each of clematis flower and myrrh, ground to powder, take one qian (3 grams) with hot wine.

Take one tai (about 15 grams) with wine, twice a day, at night blood will discharge.

Another Prescription: One liang of coix root, boiled and taken; it works after just a few doses.

  1. Blocked meridians: Take one dried silk gourd and grind it into powder, then mix it with dove's blood to form a cake. Dry and grind it daily; take two qian with empty stomach wine, first taking Four Substances Decoction for three doses. [Bencao Gangmu]

　　　　针灸

　　《甲乙经》曰：女子禁中痒，腹热痛，乳余疾，子门不端，少腹苦寒，阴痒及痛，经闭不通，中极主之。女子血不通，会阴主之。　　月水不通奔豚泄气，上下引腰脊痛，气穴主之。　　女子胞中痛，月水不以时休止，天枢主之。　　小腹胀满，痛引阴中，月水至则腰脊痛，胞中瘕，子门有寒，引髌髀痛，水道主之。　　女子月水不利，或暴闭塞，腹胀满癃，淫泺身热，腹中绞痛，(疒颓)疝阴肿，气冲针上入三寸，气至泻之。　　妇人少腹坚痛，月水不通，带脉主之。　　妇人漏下，若血闭不通：逆气胀，血海主之。　　血闭无子，不嗜食，曲泉主之。[157p]

Acupuncture

The "Jia Yi Jing" states: If a woman experiences itching in the prohibited areas, abdominal heat and pain, issues with milk secretion, improper conditions in the vaginal area, coldness and pain in the lower abdomen, and menstrual cessation, the Central Extreme point governs these conditions. If a woman's blood is not flowing, the perineum point governs her situation. If menstrual flow is obstructed, leading to distension and pain in the waist and spine, the Qi point is responsible. If there is pain within the uterus and menstrual flow does not cease at the appropriate time, the Heavenly Pivot point governs this condition. If there is distension and fullness in the lower abdomen, with pain radiating inward, resulting in pain in the waist and spine during menstruation, and if there are masses in the uterus, along with cold sensations in the vaginal area causing patellar pain, the Water Path point is responsible. If a woman experiences poor menstrual flow or sudden obstruction, with symptoms of abdominal distension, heat in the body, and cramping pain in the abdomen, along with hernias and swelling in the genital region, the Qi is pushed upwards and needs to be released. If a woman has pain and hardness in the lower abdomen along with obstructed menstrual flow, the Belt Vessel governs this issue. If there is leakage below, and if menstrual blood does not flow properly, causing counteracting Qi and distension, the Sea of Blood point is responsible. If blood is obstructed, leading to infertility and lack of appetite, the Curved Spring point governs this condition.[157p]

　　月水不利，见血而有身则败及乳肿，临泣主之。　　女子不下月水，照海主之。
　　月水不来而多闭，心下痛，目(目巟)(目巟)不可远视，水泉主之。　　《脉经》曰：左手关后尺中阳绝者，无膀胱脉也，苦逆冷，妇人月经不调，王月则闭，刺足少阴经治阴，在足内踝下动脉，即太溪穴也。　　《千金方》曰：妇人月经不断，灸内踝下白肉际脉上，随年壮。一本是青脉上。　　妇人少腹坚痛，月水不通，刺带脉入六分，灸五壮。穴在肘肋端一寸八分。　　月闭溺赤，脊强互引反折，汗不出，刺腰俞入二寸，留十呼，灸三壮。穴在第二十一椎节下间。　　月水不通，奔泄上下引腰脊痛，刺气穴、入一寸，灸五壮。穴在四满下一寸。[158p]

The monthly flow is unfavorable; if there is blood and a body present, it leads to failure and swelling of the breasts. This is governed by the "Tears of the Luteal Phase."

For women who do not have their monthly flow, it is governed by the light of the sea.

When the monthly flow does not come and there is excessive closure, there will be pain in the chest and the eyes cannot see far. This is governed by the water sources. The "Pulse Classic" states: if the left hand has a pulse in the radial artery that is absent in the bladder channel, it indicates cold and inversely troublesome conditions; if a woman’s menstruation is irregular, during Wangyue (the lunar phase), the flow will be close. One should puncture the lesser yin channel at the ankle, exactly at the Tai Xi point.

According to the "Thousand Gold Prescriptions": if a woman’s menstruation does not cease, moxibustion should be done above the white tissue of the ankle, following the year of growth. Another version states it is on the blue vein.

If a woman has a hard and painful lower abdomen, with the monthly flow not passing, needle the Dai channel for six-tenths and moxibustion for five times. The point is located an inch and eight-tenths from the elbow's rib end.

If the monthly flow is halted and urination is red, with a stiff spine and involuntary contraction leading to sweating not being produced, needle the lumbar shuru points for two inches, keeping the needle for ten breaths, moxibustion for three times. The point is located below the twenty-first vertebrae.

If the monthly flow is not circulating, leading to upper and lower leakage and pain in the waist and spine, needle the Qi point for one inch and moxibustion for five times. The point is located one inch below the fourth fullness.[158p]

　　胞中恶血，月水不以时休止，腹胀肠鸣，气上冲胸，刺天枢入五分，灸五壮。穴去盲俞一寸半。　　月水不利，见血而有身则败，乳肿，刺临泣，入二分，灸三壮。穴在足小趾次趾间，去侠豁一寸半。　　女子不下月水，痹惊善悲不乐，如堕坠，汗不出，刺照海入四分，灸二壮。穴在内踝下四分。　　《李杲十书》曰：妇人月经断绝，取四满。穴在丹田旁一寸半。　　《朱震亨心法》曰：妇人月经不调，刺窍阴三分。此穴大效，须待经定为度。在足匹指间，灸三壮。　　经闭久，忽大崩，复大绝，后又大行不调者，刺丰隆六分，止血；石门五分，断经。[159p]

If there is stagnant blood in the womb and menstrual flow does not cease timely, causing abdominal distension and bowel sounds, with qi rising to the chest, needle at the Tianshu point for five times, and moxibustion three times. This point is one and a half inches away from the Blindness point.

If the menstrual flow is not smooth and there is bleeding accompanied by a physical condition, leading to breast swelling, needle at the Linqi point for two inches, and moxibustion three times. This point is one and a half inches from the Xiāhuò point between the little toe and the next toe.

If a woman does not have menstrual flow, experiences phlegm and fright, and feels sadness and unhappiness as if in free fall, with no sweating, needle at the Zhaohai point for four inches, and moxibustion twice. This point is four inches below the inner ankle.

The "Ten Books of Li Gao" states that if a woman’s menstruation is interrupted, one should use the Sìmǎn point, located one and a half inches beside the Dantian.

The "Heart Methods of Zhu Zhenheng" states that if a woman has irregular menstruation, needle at the Qiaoyin point for three inches. This point is very effective, but one must wait until the menstrual cycle stabilizes. It is located between the two toes of the foot, moxibustion three times.

If menstruation is absent for a long time and suddenly there is heavy bleeding, then a great interruption, followed by irregular menstruation again, needle at the Fenglong point for six inches to stop the bleeding; at the Shimen point for five inches to terminate menstruation.[159p]

　　妇人五旬经断后再行，或多或少，或瘀或红并下，腹中气满如胎孕，天枢、中脘、气海各五分，立愈。　　经脉不通，已有寒热，三阴交三分，立有效。如疼时，乃经脉要通也。　　《卫生宝鉴》曰：女子不月，会阴灸三壮。穴在两阴间。　　妇人月事不利，利即多，心下满，目(目巟)(目巟)不能远视，腹中痛，可灸水泉二穴五壮。穴在内踝下。　　《医学纲目》曰：妇人经脉不通，取曲池、支沟、三里、三阴交，此四穴壅塞不通则泻之，如虚耗不行则补之。　　月经不调，取中极、三阴交、肾俞、气海。　　月经断绝，取中极、三阴交、肾俞、合谷。　　妇人通经，针合谷二分，灸三壮。穴在大指食指歧骨陷中。[160p]

After a woman’s menstrual period has ended, if there is either more or less bleeding, whether it is dark or red, and if there is fullness in the abdomen like pregnancy, acupuncture at the points Tian Shu, Zhong Wan, and Qi Hai for five minutes each will lead to a quick recovery.

If the meridians are blocked, presenting symptoms of cold and heat, needling the point San Yin Jiao for three minutes will be effective. If there is pain, it indicates that the meridians need to be unblocked.

According to the "Treasured Mirror of Health," if a woman has not menstruated for a month, moxibustion should be applied at three points on the perineum, located between the two yin areas.

If a woman’s menstrual flow is excessive and there is fullness under the heart, causing difficulty in distant vision and abdominal pain, moxibustion should be applied to the points Shui Quan for five minutes, located below the inner ankle.

According to the "Medical Principles," if a woman’s menstrual flow is obstructed, use the points Qu Chi, Zhi Gou, San Li, and San Yin Jiao. If these four points are blocked, they should be purged; if there is deficiency and stagnation, they should be tonified.

For irregular menstruation, apply needling at Zhong Ji, San Yin Jiao, Shen Shu, and Qi Hai.

For cessation of menstruation, treat with Zhong Ji, San Yin Jiao, Shen Shu, and He Gu.

To promote menstrual flow, needle He Gu for two minutes and apply moxibustion for three minutes. The point is located in the depression between the thumb and index finger.[160p]

　　月水不通，灸气冲五壮，禁针。穴在天枢下八寸动脉。　　又方：针侠溪三分，灸三壮。穴在足小指四指本节前岐骨陷中。　　又方：针会阴二寸，灸三壮。穴在肛门前前阴后，两阴间。　　月水不利，赤白带下，或身有反败，阴寒振寒，溲白，尿难痛，针行间三分，灸三壮。穴在足大指次指岐骨间。因产恶露不止，遂成疝瘕，或月事不调，血结成块，拘挛腹疝，月水不下，乳余疾绝，子阴痒，子门不端，小腹苦寒，贲豚抢心，饥不能食，腹胀，经闭不通，小便不利，及失精恍惚，尸厥烦痛，针中极一寸二分，日灸三七壮至三百壮止。穴在脐下四寸。月水不调，崩中带下，针阴交八分，日灸三七壮至七百壮止。穴在脐下一寸。[161p]

When the monthly cycle is not flowing, and there is excessive qi affecting the five organs, needles should be avoided. The acupuncture point is eight inches below the Tian Shu point on the artery.

Another method: needle the Xia Xi point three fen, and moxibustion three times. The acupuncture point is located in the depression between the fourth bone of the little toe.

Another method: needle the Hui Yin point two inches, and moxibustion three times. The acupuncture point is located at the area between the anus and the front of the perineum.

When the monthly cycle is not favorable, with red and white discharge, or with bodily backlash, coldness in the lower region, white urination, difficulty and pain in urination, needle three fen in the channel and moxibustion three times. The acupuncture point is between the first and second toes. Due to excessive postpartum discharge, hernias can develop, or menstrual irregularities, with blood clots causing abdominal and hernia contractions, unflowing monthly discharge, cessation of milk production, itching in the private area, discomfort in the lower abdomen, anger causing panic, poor appetite, abdominal distension, menstrual obstruction, difficulty with urination, loss of essence and confusion, with body numbness and pain, needle one inch and two fen deep, and perform moxibustion three times daily, totaling up to three hundred times. The acupuncture point is four inches below the navel.

For irregular monthly cycles, accompanied by irregular discharge, needle the Yin Jiao point eight fen, and perform moxibustion three times daily, totaling up to seven hundred times. The acupuncture point is one inch below the navel.[161p]

　　　　医案

　　《史记》仓公传曰：济北王侍者韩女，病腰背痛，寒热。众医皆以为寒热也。臣意诊脉曰：内寒，月事不下也，即窜以药，旋下病已。病得之欲男子而不可得也。所以知韩女之病者，诊其脉时，切之肾脉也，濇而不属。濇而不属者，其来难坚，故曰：月事不下。肝脉弦出左口，故曰欲男子不可得也。盖男子以精为主，妇人以血为主。男子精盛则思室，女子月盛则怀胎。夫肝，摄血者也。厥阴弦出寸部，又上鱼际，则阴血盛可知也。[162p]

Medical Case

In the "Records of the Historian," it is said in the biography of Cang Gong: The maid of King Jibei, Han Nü, suffered from pain in her waist and back, along with chills and fevers. All the doctors believed it to be due to chills and fevers. However, in my opinion, upon examining her pulse, I found internal coldness, and that her menstrual flow had not occurred. Thus, I treated her with medicine, and soon after, her condition improved. The root of her illness was her desire for a male offspring which she could not obtain. Therefore, I discerned the nature of Han Nü's ailment by examining her pulse and found it weak and unsteady at the kidney pulse. The weak and unsteady pulse indicates that it is difficult to establish a regular pattern, thus the menstrual flow has not come. The liver pulse was tense at the left side, indicating her desire for a son was unattainable. It is because men are primarily associated with essence, while women are primarily associated with blood. When a man's essence is abundant, he thinks of establishing a household; when a woman's blood is plentiful, she is capable of conceiving. The liver is responsible for regulating blood. The Jueyin pulse is tense at the wrist and extends to the thenar eminence, indicating that the yin blood is abundant.[162p]

　　《元史》曰：裴泽之妻病寒热，月事不至者数年，已喘嗽矣，医者率以蛤蚧、桂、附之药投之。李杲曰：不然。夫入病阴为阳所搏，温剂太过，故无益而反害，投以寒血之药则经行矣。已而果然。
　　《儒门事亲》曰：一妇月事不行，寒热往来，口干颊赤，喜饮，旦暮间咳一二声。诸医皆云经血不行，宜蝱虫、水蛭、干漆、硇砂、芫青、红娘子、没药、血竭之类。惟戴人不然，曰：古方中虽有此法，奈病人服之，必腹脐发痛，饮食不进。乃命止药，饮食稍进。《内经》曰：二阳之病发心脾。心受之则血不流，故女子不月。既心受积热，宜抑火升水，流湿润燥，开胃进食，乃涌出痰一二升，下泄水五六行。湿水上下皆去，血气自行，月事不为水湿所隔，自依期而至矣。亦不用蝱虫、水蛭有毒之药，如用之，则月经纵来，小溲反闭，他证生矣。凡精血不足，当补之以食，大忌有毒之药偏胜而致夭枉。[163p]

The "Yuan History" states: Pei Ze’s wife suffered from chills and fevers, her menstrual cycle was absent for several years, and she developed a cough. The doctors generally prescribed medicines containing gecko, cinnamon, and aconite. Li Gao disagreed, saying: It is a case where the yang attacks the yin, and excessive warming agents are ineffective and even harmful; using cold-blooded medicines will restore her menstrual flow. Eventually, this proved to be true.

The "Confucian Door to Filial Piety" mentions a woman whose menstruation was absent, experiencing alternating chills and fevers, dry mouth, red cheeks, a thirst for drink, and a cough once or twice during the day and night. All doctors diagnosed her as having stagnant menstrual blood and prescribed the likes of gall insects, leeches, lacquer, pounded stone, wild rue, and myrrh. Only Dai Ren disagreed, stating: Although ancient prescriptions include these remedies, patients who take them are bound to experience abdominal pain and loss of appetite. He then ordered to stop the medicines and gradually allowed food intake.

The "Inner Canon" states: When both forms of yang disease affect the heart and spleen, if the heart is afflicted, the blood does not flow, hence the woman’s menstruation is absent. Once the heart accumulates heat, one should reduce fire and promote water to flow, moistening dryness and stimulating appetite, which will then cause the discharge of one or two liters of phlegm and several flows of water. Humidity will dissipate, allowing blood and qi to move freely, leading to the restoration of menstruation on schedule without being obstructed by dampness.

There is no need to use toxic substances like gall insects or leeches; if used, even if menstruation returns, small urination may be hindered, and other symptoms will arise. Whenever there is a deficiency of vital blood, it should be replenished through diet, and one must avoid toxic medicines that could lead to fatal consequences.[163p]

　　一妇年三十四岁，经水不行，寒热往来，面色痿黄，唇焦颊赤，时咳三两声，同者所服之药，黑神散、乌金丸、四物汤、烧肝散、鳖甲散、建中汤、宁肺散，针艾百千，病转剧。家人意倦，不欲求治。戴人悯之，先涌痰五六升，午前涌毕，午后进食，余证悉除。后三日，复轻涌之，又去痰一二升，食益进。不数日，又下通经散，泻讫一二升，后数日去死皮数重，小者如麸片，大者如苇膜。不一月，经水行，神气大安矣。[164p]

A woman, thirty-four years old, had irregular menstruation, alternating cold and heat, a pale yellow complexion, with dry lips and a flushed face. She occasionally coughed a few times. The medications she had previously taken included Black God Powder, Black Gold Pill, Siwu Decoction, Liver Burn Powder, Turtle Shell Powder, Jianzhong Decoction, and Ningfei Powder, along with hundreds of acupuncture sessions, but her condition worsened. Her family, feeling weary, did not wish to seek further treatment. A compassionate individual intervened, first draining five or six liters of phlegm. By noon, the draining was complete, and in the afternoon she began to eat, with all other symptoms eliminated. Three days later, phlegm was lightly drained again, and one or two liters were removed, after which her appetite improved. In a few days, she was given a menstrual regulation powder, which resulted in the expulsion of one or two liters. In the following days, a significant amount of dead skin was shed, some pieces as small as bran flakes and others as large as reed membranes. Within a month, her menstruation resumed, and her spirit was greatly improved.[164p]

　　一妇人年二十余岁，病经闭不行，寒热往来，咳嗽潮热，庸医禁切，无物可食。一日，当暑出门，忽见卖凉粉者，以冰水和饮，大为一食，顿觉神清骨健，数月，经水自下。
　　《丹溪心法》曰：一妇人久疟，食少经闭。两手无脉，每日与三花神佑丸十余粒，津咽之，月余食进脉出，又半月遂愈，又一月经行。
　　《医学纲目》曰：一妇人三十岁，每因浴后，必用冷水淋通身，又尝大惊，遂患经来时必先少腹大痛，口吐涎水，然后经行，行后又吐水二日，其痛直至六七日经水止时方住，百药不效。予诊其脉，寸滑大而弦，关尺皆弦大而急，尺小于关，关小于寸，所谓前大后小也。遂用香附三两，半夏二两，茯苓、黄芩各一两半，枳实、延胡、丹皮、人参、当归、白朮、桃仁各一两，黄连七钱，川楝、远志、甘草各半两，桂三钱，茱萸一钱半，分十五贴，水煎，入生姜汁两蚬壳，热服，后用热汤洗浴，得微汗乃已。[165p]

A woman in her twenties suffered from amenorrhea, alternating chills and fever, and coughing with tidal fever. Mediocre doctors forbade her from eating anything, leaving her with nothing to consume. One day, as summer approached, she went out and unexpectedly saw a seller of cold jelly. She mixed it with ice water and consumed a large quantity, immediately feeling refreshed and invigorated. After several months, her menstruation resumed.

The "Danxi Heart Method" states: A woman with prolonged malaria experienced little food and amenorrhea. Her pulse was weak, and every day she took over ten pills of Sanhua Shenyou pills, swallowing them with saliva. After a month, her appetite and pulse improved; after another half month, she fully recovered, and after one more month, her menstruation returned.

The "Medical Essentials" mentions: A woman aged thirty always experienced a cold water shower after bathing. After a great shock, she suffered severe lower abdominal pain before her menstruation, followed by excessive salivation, and only then did her menstruation come. Afterward, she would vomit for two days, and the pain lasted until the seventh or sixth day when her menstruation ceased, and no medicines had any effect. I examined her pulse; it was slippery and large at the cun position but taut; the guan and chi positions were both taut, large, and rapid, with the chi smaller than the guan, and the guan smaller than the cun, which indicates the front is larger than the back. I then prescribed three liang of Xiangfu, two liang of Banxia, one and a half liang each of Fuling and Huangqin, one liang each of Zhishi, Yanhusuo, Danpi, Ren Shen, Dang Gui, Bai Zhu, and Tao Ren, seven qian of Huanglian, and half a liang each of Chuanlian, Yuan Zhi, and Gancao, with three qian of Guo and one and a half qian of Zhuyou. This was divided into fifteen doses, boiled in water, combined with two shreds of fresh ginger juice, and taken hot. Afterwards, she was to bathe with hot soup until slightly sweating, then stop.[165p]

忌当风坐卧、手足见水并吃生冷。服三十贴全愈。半年后，又因惊忧，前病复举，腰腹时痛，小便淋痛，心惕惕跳惊悸，予意其表已解，病独在里，先与灸少冲、劳宫、昆仑、三阴交四穴，止悸定痛；次用桃仁承气大下之；下后用香附三两，蓬朮、当归各一两半，三棱、延胡索、肉桂、大黄、青皮俱酢制、青木香、茴香、滑石、木通，桃仁各一两，乌药、甘草、砂仁、槟榔、苦楝肉各半两，木香、吴茱萸各二钱，分作二十贴，入新取牛膝湿者二钱，生姜五片，用荷叶汤煎服，服讫渐安。[166p]

Avoid sitting or lying in the wind, having hands and feet exposed to water, and eating raw or cold foods. After applying thirty medicinal patches, a full recovery was achieved. Six months later, due to anxiety and worry, the previous illness relapsed, causing pain in the lower back and abdomen, painful urination, and a feeling of palpitations and anxiety. I believed the surface symptoms had resolved but the underlying issue remained. First, I applied moxibustion to the points Shaochong, Laogong, Kunlun, and Sanyinjiao to stop the palpitations and ease the pain. Next, I used Tao Ren (peach kernel) to induce a strong downward movement. After the treatment, I used three taels of Xiangfu, one and a half taels each of Poria and Angelica, and one tael each of Sanleng, Yanhusuo, Cinnamon, Rhubarb, and Qingpi, all prepared with vinegar. Additionally, one tael each of Qingmuxiang, Fennel, Talcum, and Mutong, along with one tael of Tao Ren, half a tael each of Wuyao, Ganjiang, Sand ginger, Betel nut, and Bitter neem, and two qian (drachms) each of Muxiang and Wuzhuyu were divided into twenty patches. I combined this with two qian of freshly collected Niu Xi (Achyranthes) and five slices of fresh ginger, decocting with lotus leaf tea for consumption. Gradually, the patient felt at ease after completing the treatment.[166p]

　　陈氏妇二十余岁，形肥痞塞不食，每日卧至未牌，吃一盏薄粥，吃粥后必吐水半碗仍复卧，经不通三月矣。前番曾暗通，黑色。脉之，辰时寸关滑而有力，午后关滑寸不滑；询之，因乘怒饮食而然。遂以白朮一两半，厚朴、黄连、枳实各一两，半夏、茯苓、陈皮，山楂、人参、滑石各八钱，砂仁、香附、桃仁各半两，红花二钱，分作十贴，每日服一贴，各入姜汁二蚬壳；间三日，以神佑丸、神秘沉香丸微下之，至十二日吐止、食渐进；四十日平复如故。[167p]

The Chen woman, over twenty years old, was stout and felt bloated, her appetite poor. She would lie in bed until late morning, consuming a bowl of thin porridge daily, but afterwards would inevitably vomit up half a bowl and return to bed. Her bowels had not functioned for three months. Previously, there had been hidden connections, dark in nature. Upon pulse examination, her pulse at the hour of Chen was slippery and strong, while in the afternoon it was slippery but weak; when inquired, she explained it was due to an episode of anger leading her to overeat. Thus, I prescribed one and a half taels of Baizhu, one tael each of Houpo, Huanglian, and Zhi Shi, eight qian each of Banxia, Fuling, Chenpi, Hawthorn, Ren Shen, and Huashi, half a tael each of Sharen, Xiangfu, and Taoren, and two qian of Honghua, divided into ten doses, with each dose mixed with two drops of ginger juice; after three days, I administered Shenyou Wan and Shenmi Chenxiang Wan to gently purgative her. By the twelfth day, her vomiting ceased and her appetite gradually returned; after forty days, she returned to her usual state.[167p]

　　《薛己医案》曰：一少妇耳下患肿，素勤苦，发热口干，月水每过期而至，且少。一老媪以为经闭，用水蛭之类通之，以致愈虚而毙。夫月水之为物，乃手太阳手少阴二经主之，此二经相为表里，主上为乳汁，下为月水，为经络之余气。苟外无六淫所侵，内无七情所伤，脾胃之气壮，则冲任之气盛，故为月水，适时而至。然而面色痿黄，四肢消瘦，发热口干，月水过期且少，乃阴血不足也。非有余瘀闭之证，宜以滋养血气之剂，徐而培之，则经气盛而经水自依时而下。一妇人经候过期，发热倦怠，或用四物、黄连之类，反两月一度，且少而成块；又用峻药通之，两目如帛所蔽。予诊之曰：脾为诸阴之首，目为血脉之宗，此脾伤五脏皆为失所，不能归于目矣。遂用补中益气、济生归脾二汤，专主脾胃，年余寻愈。[168p]

The "Medical Case of Xue Ji" states: A young woman experienced swelling below her ear, suffered from frequent heat and dry mouth, and had her menstrual flow come late and in small amounts. An elderly woman, thinking it was due to menstrual closure, used leeches to treat it, which led to her becoming weaker and eventually dying. The menstrual flow is governed by the hand Taiyang and hand Shaoyin meridians, which are interrelated; one governs milk and the other governs menstrual flow, as they are the residual energy of the meridians. If there is no invasion of the six excesses from the outside, and no injury from the seven emotions on the inside, and if the spleen and stomach's energy is strong, then the Chong and Ren vessels will be abundant, causing the menstrual flow to arrive at the proper time. However, with a pale yellow complexion, emaciated limbs, heat and dry mouth, and menstruation that is overdue and scant, there is a deficiency of yin and blood. This is not due to an excess of blood stasis but rather indicates the need for nourishing blood and energy. Gradually nurturing it will ensure the menstrual energy becomes robust and the flow arrives on time.

There was a woman whose menstrual cycle was overdue, and she experienced fever and fatigue. She used formulas such as Si Wu and Huang Lian, but after two months, the flow was still scant and clotty; moreover, using harsh drugs to expedite it caused her eyes to appear as if covered by silk. I diagnosed that the spleen is the chief of all yin, and the eyes are the root of the blood vessels. If the spleen is damaged, all the organs will lose their proper function and cannot return to the eyes. Thus, I used the formulas Bu Zhong Yi Qi and Ji Sheng Gui Pi, focusing on strengthening the spleen and stomach. After a year, she recovered.[168p]

　　一妇人发热口干，月经不调，两腿无力；或用袪风渗湿之剂，腿痛体倦，二膝浮肿，经事不通。余作足三阴经血虚火燥，名鹤膝风。用六味、八味二丸兼服两月，形体渐健，饮食渐进，膝肿渐消，半载而痊。
　　一妇人月事未期而至，发热自汗，或用清热止汗之剂，作渴头眩，手掉身麻。余曰：此肝经血虚火动，火为阳，阳盛则生风，用柴胡、炒芩、连、山栀、归、芍、生地、丹皮各一钱，参、芪、苓、朮各一钱五分，川芎七分，甘草五分。二剂汗止；用补中益气汤而愈。
　　一妇人经行劳役，忽然昏愦，面赤吐痰。余曰：此乃去血过多。阳无所附故耳。急饮童便碗许，神思渐爽；更用参、芪各五钱，芎、归各三钱，元参、柴胡、山栀、炙甘草各一钱，一剂；又用逍遥散加五味、麦门二剂，如此月余渐愈。但体倦面黄，又以十全大补加五味、麦冬治之而愈。若投以发散之剂，祸在反掌，慎之！[169p]

A woman had fever and dry mouth, with irregular menstruation and weak legs; after using a remedy to dispel wind and eliminate dampness, she experienced leg pain and fatigue, with swollen knees and obstruction of menstruation. Another woman had her period arrive prematurely, experiencing fever and sweating. 　　一妇人素勤苦，冬初患咳嗽发热，久而吐血盗汗，经水两三月一至，遍身作痛，或用化痰降火药，口噤筋挛，此血虚而药益损耳。用加减八味丸及补中益气，加麦门、五味、山药治之，年余而愈。
　　一妇人性沉多虑，月经不行，胸满少食，或作胀，或吞酸，余以为中气虚寒，用补中益气加砂仁、香附、煨姜二剂，胸膈和而饮食进。更以六君加芎、归、贝母、桔梗、生姜、大枣数剂，脾胃健而经自调矣。
　　一妇人素有胃火，或用清胃散而安，后因劳役，躁渴内热，肌肉消瘦，月经不行，余谓此胃火消烁阴血，用逍遥散加丹皮、炒栀以清胃热，用八珍汤如茯苓、远志以养脾血，而经自行。
　　一妇人久患疟，形体怯弱，内热晡热，自汗盗汗，饮食少思，月事不行，或用通经丸，虚证悉具。余曰：此因虚而致疟，因疟以闭经也。用补中益气及六味地黄丸各百余剂，疟愈而经自行。[170p]

A woman had long suffered from hardship. At the beginning of winter, she developed a cough and fever. After a long time, she coughed up blood and experienced night sweats. 　　一妇人生七胎矣，月经不调，两足发热，年余而身亦热，劳则足酸痛；又年余，唇肿裂痛；又半年，唇裂见血，形体瘦倦，饮食无味，月水不通，唇下肿如黑枣，或用通经丸等药而死。
　　儒者钱思习子室，年三十余无嗣，月经淋沥无期，夫妇异处几年矣。思习欲为娶妾，以谋诸余。余意此郁怒伤肝脾，虚火功而血不归经，乃肝不能藏，脾不能摄也。当清肝火补脾气，遂与加味归脾、逍遥二药四剂，送至其家，仍告其姑曰：服此病自愈而当受胎，妾可无娶也。病果愈，次年生子。
　　一妇人性急，每怒非太阳耳项喉齿胸乳作痛，则胸满吞酸，吐泻少食，经行不止，此皆肝火之证，肝自病则外证见，土受克则内证作，余先以四物加白朮、茯苓、柴胡、炒栀、炒龙胆，清肝养血，次用四君加柴胡、芍药、神曲、吴茱萸、炒黄连以培土制肝，渐愈。惟月经不止，是血分有热，脾气尚虚，以逍遥散倍用白朮、茯苓、陈皮，又以补中益气加酒炒芍药兼服而安。[171p]

A woman had seven pregnancies, her menstrual cycle was irregular, her legs were warm, and for over a year, she felt heat throughout her body, and her feet ached when fatigued. After another year, her lips swelled, cracked, and hurt; after another six months, her lips split and bled, her body became thin and fatigued, her appetite diminished, her menstrual flow ceased, and the area beneath her lips swelled like black dates, sometimes resulting in death from taking medicines like menstrual regulating pills.

The Confucian scholar Qian Sixi had no descendants after more than thirty years. His wife's menstrual flow was intermittent, and they had lived apart for several years. Qian Sixi wished to take a concubine to seek heirs. I believed this was due to anger and sorrow harming the liver and spleen, causing empty heat leading to blood not returning to the menstrual cycle, thus the liver could not store and the spleen could not hold. I decided to clear liver heat and tonify spleen qi, so I provided him with a modified Gui Pi and Xiao Yao formula in four doses, which I sent to his home, advising his mother-in-law that taking this would cure her condition and she could conceive without needing to marry another wife. Indeed, the ailment was resolved, and the following year, he had a child.

A woman was naturally impatient; whenever she was angry, her temples, throat, teeth, chest, and breasts would ache. This caused fullness in her chest, sour belching, and she would have little appetite and continuous menstrual flow. These were all signs of liver fire. When the liver was in disorder, external signs appeared; when the earth was overwhelmed, internal signs emerged. I first used Si Wu Decoction with Bai Zhu, Fu Ling, Chai Hu, Stir-fried Zhi Zi, and Stir-fried Long Dan to clear the liver and nourish blood, then I applied Si Jun Zi Tang with Chai Hu, Shao Yao, Shen Qu, Wu Zhu Yu, and Stir-fried Huang Lian to strengthen the earth and control the liver, gradually improving her condition. However, the menstruation was still ongoing, indicating that the blood had heat and the spleen qi was still deficient, so I used Xiao Yao San with increased Bai Zhu, Fu Ling, and Chen Pi, and also incorporated Bu Zhong Yi Qi Tang with wine-fried Shao Yao for concurrent use to stabilize her condition.[171p]

　　一妇人多怒，经行旬余方止，后淋沥无期，肌体倦瘦，口干内热，盗汗如洗，日晡热甚，皆由肝脾亏损，无以生发元气，用参、芪、归、朮、茯神、远志、枣仁、麦门、五味、丹皮、龙眼肉、炙甘草、柴胡、升麻治之，获痊。此证先因怒动肝火，血热妄行，后乃脾气下陷，不能摄血归源，故用前药。若胃热亡津液而经不行，宜清胃。若心火亢甚者，宜清心。若服燥药过多者，宜养血。若病久气血衰，宜健脾胃。
　　一妇人怀抱不舒，腹胀少寐，饮食素少，痰涎上涌，月经频数。余曰：脾统血而主涎。此郁闷伤脾，不能摄血归源耳。用补中益气、济生归脾而愈。
　　一室女年十七，疬久不愈，天癸未通，发热咳嗽，饮食少思，欲用通经丸。余曰：此盖因禀气不足，阴血未充故耳，但养气血，益津液，其经自行。彼惑于速效，仍用之。余曰：非其治也。此乃慓悍之剂，大助阳火，阴血得之则妄行，脾胃得之则愈虚。后果经血妄行，饮食愈少，遂致不救。[172p]

　　一妇人面黄或赤，时觉腰间或脐下作痛，四肢困倦，烦热不安，其经若行，先发寒热，两肋如束，其血如崩。此脾胃虚损，元气下陷，与相火湿热所致。用补中益气汤加防风、芍药、炒黑黄蘗，间以归脾汤调其化源，血自归经矣。
　　一妇人经行腹痛，食则呕吐，肢体倦怠，发热作渴，此乃素禀气血不足，用八珍汤二十余剂而愈。后生子二年而经不行，前证仍作，服八珍汤、逍遥散百余剂方愈。
　　一妇人年五十，内热晡热，经水两三月一至，此血虚有热，用逍遥散加山茱萸治之而愈。后有痰作渴，或小便不调，或头运白带，用六味丸而安。
　　一妇人晡热。肢体瘦倦，食少无味，月经不行，或鼻衄或血崩半载矣。或用顺气饮子清热止血等剂，不应，更加寒热，且时欲呕。余以为郁怒亏损脾胃，虚火错经妄行而然耳。遂朝用补中益气汤，夕用六味地黄丸各数剂，半载而痊。[173p]

　　一妇人性素沉静，晡热内热，月经不调，后每一二月或齿缝或舌下或咽间出血碗许，如此年余，服清热凉血调理之药益甚，问治于予。予谓肝脾气郁，血热上行，先用加味归脾汤，后用加味逍遥散，摄血归源而经自调，前证顿愈。一室女久患寒热，月经不调，先以小柴胡加生地治之少愈，更以生地黄丸而痊。
　　一妇人因怒，寒热头疼，讝言妄语，至夜益甚，月经暴至，此怒动肝火，用加味逍遥散加生地黄治之，神思顿清。但食少体倦，月经未已，盖脾统血，此脾气虚不能摄血，用补中益气汤而痊。
　　《证治准绳》曰：一妇人瘦小，年二十余，经水紫色，或前或后，临行腹痛，恶寒喜热，或时感寒，腹亦作痛，脉皆细濡近滑，两尺重按，略洪而滑，此血热也。或谓：恶寒如此，何谓为热？曰：热极似寒也。遂用酒煮黄连四两，香附、归身尾各二两，五灵脂一两，为末粥丸，空服吞之而愈。[174p]

The "Principles of Diagnosis and Treatment" states: A woman, small and thin, around twenty years old, had dark purple menstrual blood that was irregular, experiencing abdominal pain before and during menstruation, with a dislike for cold yet craving warmth. Sometimes she would have chills, and her abdomen would hurt again, with a pulse that was thin, moist, and slightly slippery, with a heavy yet slightly full feeling on the pulse.
